Jeffrey Yip< /Name>
<Time>1433038956577</Time>< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
Excellent food. The steampot dish is a must eat. All yakitori items are just plain delicious.

UPDATE.  AMAZING! And they just got better with their lunch specials! No one, I say, no one is doing what they're doing right now: high quality food, authentic options, and all for $10 in a bento box. The bento special comes with a big salad, a large portion of rice, and miso soup. You can choose two items from such Japanese true staples as takoyaki (fried octopus balls with seaweed powder, bonita fish flakes, and teriyaki sauce), gyoza (best in the Tri-Valley), salmon teriyaki, Japanese croquettes (fried potato cakes) and chicken karaage (deep-fried boneless chicken to die for). Come eat for lunch and dinner (the kushiyaki grill sampler is the number one choice and best deal) and just enjoy. On weekends, for now you can avoid the lunch crowds. Good food, great pricing, and clean and friendly service. And don't forget to ask for Ramune to wash it down with all your favorite dishes!< /text>
